The Fruit Industry Association sent a letter through the County Chamber of Commerce to the General Headquarters, vouching for Geng's peaceful nature and requesting that he be exempted from further investigation, as he had no communist suspicions.

Wuxi 99

Brutal Husband Kills Wife, Buries Body, and Attempts to Conceal Evidence: In Chen Douban Lane, Zhuang Chen Township, District 5 (Tianshang City) of the county, a villager named Chen Quangen was a carpenter. His family was poor. His wife, Lu (also known as A Qiao), was nearly forty years old and suffered from a mental illness, acting like a madwoman and speaking incoherently. They had two sons and one daughter: the eldest son named Jin Fu, the second son named Jin Sheng, and the daughter named A Mei. The eldest son currently works as a waiter in a restaurant near Huangbu Pier. Chen Quangen saw that his wife was demented and practically useless. Therefore, the relationship between husband and wife was very bad. On the evening of the 29th of last month, Chen Quangen suddenly had the idea to kill her. He killed Lu with a wooden object and moved the body to a mulberry field next to the Tangtou Education Hall. He dug a muddy pit and buried her naked, intending to conceal the evidence. The next day, villagers became suspicious because Chen Lu suddenly disappeared. They inquired with Chen Quangen, who sent his younger brother, Chen Panlao, hurrying to the city. He summoned his nephew, Jin Fu, to the countryside. They searched everywhere and even dredged the nearby river, but found no trace. It wasn't until the 5th of this month that Lu's body was found in the soil in the mulberry field next to the Education Hall. Thereupon, the son of the deceased, Chen Jinfu, together with You Pinshan, the head of the 21st Tu (a local administrative unit), reported to the County Court, requesting an examination. Upon receiving the report, the Prosecutor's Office had Prosecutor Shen conduct an interrogation. Because the testimony of the Tu head was confusing, he was ordered to post bail. Chen Jinfu was ordered to return home. The murderer, Chen Quangen, had escaped at the time, but was apprehended by his younger brother, Chen Panlao, at Zhoujing Corridor in Zhoujing Lane and sent to the police station of the 12th Public Security Sub-bureau for temporary custody. Yesterday (the 7th), Prosecutor Shen, along with Coroner Wang and court police, went to the scene of the crime to conduct a legal examination. The examination revealed that the deceased, Chen Lu, had slight discoloration over her entire body, and it was confirmed that she had been buried alive. After the examination, the family was ordered to prepare a coffin for burial. The murderer, Chen Quangen, was taken to the court for interrogation and custody, pending investigation.

Changzhou 100

Benniu Police and Militia Encircle and Suppress Bandits: A Changzhou-bound boat from Lvcheng Town, Danyang, was robbed by bandits on the morning of the 5th in the canal near Benniu. Upon learning of this, the Second Public Security Sub-bureau rushed to suppress and capture them. The bandits opened fire, and there was a long exchange of gunfire. Then, the nearby militia crossed the river to provide support and jointly encircled and suppressed the bandits. The bandits were dispersed, and a large amount of stolen goods was recovered. On the 6th, the police were dispatched to search for the remaining stolen goods, which were then returned to the victim, Wu Yuxiao.

Jiangyin 101

Murder Case Occurs in Shengang Township: Wu Arong, a farmer in Shengfeng Village, Shengang Township, District 5, was hacked to death with an axe on the morning of the 5th. The body was thrown into a field on the edge of a well. Villagers discovered the body and reported it to the district office, which then reported it to the county. The county sent Trial Officer Wang Cheng to the village to conduct an examination. The deceased's head had been hacked five times with an axe, and his left hand had been hacked three times, with his fingers chopped off. According to the deceased's wife, Wu Tang, the deceased was hacked to death by his uncle, Wu Jisheng, due to land disputes and long-standing hatred. Wu Jisheng was summoned for questioning but denied the charges. He will be taken to the county for further investigation.

They pried open the door and tied up the entire family with ropes, guarded by one bandit. The remaining bandits rushed into the bedroom and searched it thoroughly. It is estimated that they stole cash, silver, and gold jewelry worth about three to four hundred yuan.

Pinghu 103

Gambler Robbed on Way Home from Gambling Den: An elderly man named Yao from the South Gate won over a hundred silver dollars from a gambling den the other night and was carrying them home. When he reached the vicinity of the South Temple, four men suddenly emerged from the darkness and knocked Yao to the ground. They snatched the silver dollars and fled into Shi Lane. Ningbo 104

Yu Youren Tours Baima Lake: Yu Youren, a member of the Central Committee and President of the Control Yuan of the National Government, traveled from Nanjing to Yu on the 2nd of this month with Central Committee member Jing Hengyi. Tong Hanchun Store Owner's Home Robbed: The home of Tong Sanyu and Tong Yougu in Zhuangqiao, Cixi, who runs the Tong Hanchun Pharmacy in Shanghai, is wealthy. The ancestral house is very large, and only Yougu's father and several female relatives live there. Yesterday at midnight, seven bandits armed with fake pistols, rakes, and hoes broke into the house and robbed it. They stole a pearl and gem ring worth over 2,000 yuan, a pearl circle worth 200 yuan, paper money worth 450 yuan, and gold jewelry, resulting in a total loss of over 3,000 yuan.

Xia Shantai Fire in Xiaoshan Kills Two: 105

The home of farmer Shen Guiyuan in Xia Shantai, Xiaoshan, caught fire on the night of the 6th due to mosquito coils igniting the grass. In an instant, thick smoke rose up, and because the neighbors had no fire-fighting equipment, they had to let it spread. The fire burned from 11:00 PM to 1:00 AM, destroying three two-story buildings, five single-story buildings, and two thatched sheds. A three-year-old girl and a sixty-year-old woman were burned to death. The remaining clothing and utensils were completely destroyed, with losses exceeding ten thousand yuan.

Educational News

Important News

Various Locations 106

Celebrating Teachers' Day 107

Capital City: The Teachers' Day Commemoration Assembly in the capital city was held at 2:00 PM on June 6th in the auditorium of Jinling University. Over two hundred teachers from various schools attended (including those from Central University, Jinling University, Jinling Women's University, Cultural Institute, Nanjing Middle School, Nanjing Women's Middle School, Zhongying Middle School, Dongfang Middle School, Qingzhong Middle School, Central District Experimental School, and all elementary schools in Nanjing). Zhang Shi gave an opening speech, encouraging teachers to promote frugality, possess a specialized spirit, engage in self-cultivation, and exercise their bodies. Peng Baichuan reported on the preparations for the assembly, stating that this was the second assembly this year, initiated by Shao Shulong last year at Central University, and discussed important matters. Luo Tingguang from the university, Li Qingsong from the middle school, and Wang Zhixiang from the elementary school gave speeches successively. Resolutions were passed regarding safeguarding the status of teachers, enhancing teachers' self-cultivation, and improving teachers' salaries. A declaration was also issued.

Local News

Shanghai Will Not Hold Them Temporarily

Middle and Primary School Examinations 109

Zhejiang Province's secondary school examinations will also be held later, and primary schools, which have always had examinations, will still conduct them this year.

Shanghai: According to a recent report, the city will hold graduation examinations for middle and primary schools on a scheduled basis. A reporter from the Education Society visited the person in charge of the Municipal Education Bureau to inquire about the examination methods. According to them, the bureau, after receiving the graduation examination regulations for middle and primary schools issued by the Ministry of Education, was considering them but had not yet decided whether to hold them. Later, because the city was located in a war zone, the schools were affected by the war, and the start of the school year varied. Various subjects could not be completed at the same time. Therefore, the graduation examinations for middle and primary schools this summer vacation will be temporarily suspended. A report has been submitted to the Ministry of Education for verification and instructions.

Zhejiang Province: The Zhejiang Provincial Department of Education received an order from the Ministry of Education, stipulating the graduation examination methods for middle and primary schools. It should have complied with the order and held the examinations this semester. However, the document from the Ministry arrived late, and the summer vacation was approaching. The public and private middle schools in the province were about to hold graduations, and there was insufficient time to prepare. Furthermore, the first time holding examinations should be handled with caution to ensure completion. A report has been submitted to the Ministry of Education requesting instructions on postponing the graduation examinations for middle school students this semester. As for primary school graduates, various counties and cities have always held examinations. The Department of Education has issued a notice to all counties and cities to follow the Ministry's order and organize examination committees to handle them separately. If they cannot be held this semester, they should state their reasons and submit them to the Department for verification.

Cai Yuanpei Mediates the Student Unrest at China Public School 110

| Today's Board of Directors Meeting |

| Students Temporarily Suspend Classes |

According to the National Society, Cai Yuanpei, President of the National Central Research Institute, returned to Nanjing from Wuhan a few days ago and immediately received a telegram from the board of directors of the Shanghai China Public School University, informing him that the student unrest at the school was complex and could not be resolved without the chairman of the board (Cai) personally coming to Shanghai. After receiving the telegram, Cai took the overnight express train to Shanghai the night before last and is scheduled to convene a board of directors meeting today to mediate everything. It was also announced that students would temporarily suspend classes until the dispute is resolved.

Youth Handball Competition 113

Begins on the 20th of this month

Registration closes on the 18th

In recent years, ball sports such as soccer and tennis in our country have made considerable progress, but handball has rarely been heard of. Even in Shanghai, few people pay attention to it. However, its effectiveness in strengthening the body and its interest are not inferior to tennis, and its cost is several times less than practicing tennis. Therefore, in recent years, various schools and public sports organizations have slightly promoted it. However, to improve skills, more competitions are necessary. In view of this, the Youth Association has launched the Shanghai Youth Association Open Handball Competition, divided into doubles and singles events. The regulations are as follows:

(1) Registration period: from now until the 18th of this month

(2) Registration fee: free for members, 20 cents per person for non-members

(3) Competition date: starts from the 20th of this month, with games starting at 5:30 PM daily

(4) Competition method: the elimination or round-robin system will be determined based on the number of participants. The competition order will be determined by the committee through drawing lots

(5) Competition balls: the balls used in the competition will be provided by this department to ensure uniformity

(6) Absence rules: players must appear at the scheduled time, with a grace period of five minutes. If they are late beyond that, it will be considered a loss. However, this does not apply if there is a valid reason, the opponent has been contacted in advance, and the sports department has been notified to postpone the match one day before the competition

(7) Competition officials: all officials in the competition will be appointed by this department

(8) Arbitrator's powers: the arbitrator's powers are to resolve issues related to serving, returning the ball, whether the ball lands inside or outside the court, whether the ball is obstructed or in error, and to resolve disputes not covered by the rules

(9) Recorder's responsibility: specifically to record wins, losses, and points and report everything

(10) Prizes: the committee will decide after the registration is closed

Shanghai Education After the January 28th Incident (10) (2) Shang 119

Nineteen Recent Schools

On March 1st, our army defended the second line of defense, and the war came to an end. The people of Shanghai temporarily stopped hearing gunfire and artillery. The frightened people gradually woke up. Parents wanted to send their children to school, teachers worked even harder in schools, and students felt that long-term absenteeism was not a good policy. Closed schools planned to reopen, and the number of students in schools that had already opened gradually increased. On March 16th, the Joint Association of Teachers and Staff of the China School issued a letter of encouragement to all schools to resume classes. Their reason was that since the enemy had accumulated decades of ambition to plot against us, the resistant actions against the enemy could not be stopped in a short time. We citizens must be calm, those who work should settle into their jobs, and those who study should settle into their studies, in order to cope with the long term. Education is the foundation of the country. Yue Wang Goujian used it to defeat Wu, and the Japanese used it to show their strength. We were brought to a poor and weak position due to the stagnation of education. Now the concession in the southern city is peaceful and quiet, and the melting spring scenery is the time for our youth to study hard. Please, patriotic teachers and students, temporarily endure the pain, calm your minds, invigorate your spirits, and quickly open school and start classes. Use twelve points of effort to seek practical scientific education to consolidate the national foundation for resisting foreign aggression. Such a proposition is indeed very important in times of chaos.

The ceasefire agreement was signed on May 5th, the anniversary of the revolutionary government, the day Sun Yat-sen took office as the extraordinary president. The air on all sides shows the image of clear skies after the rain and the earth returning to spring. Schools, of course, work hard to open their doors for the country and for the family. Even 90% of the private schools burned in the war zone have set up stoves, arranged desks and chairs, and started ringing the bells. Don't you see the brand new blue characters on a white background and white characters on a black background, almost every five steps and every ten steps, hanging high and majestically in the concession? The poor Pudong Middle School, Dongwu Second Middle School, and Danhua Middle School are still tightly closed for some reason. The classroom chairs are covered with dust, as if they have been exhausted by oppression and have no courage to struggle anymore.

The Municipal Wuben Girls' Middle School, full of talented people, will restore its old appearance. Jingye Middle School, Xinlu Normal School, and Wusong Middle School are working together to make a fake

are merging with Chengdu Road and An Elementary School to hold classes, but there are less than 170 students, a decrease of two-thirds compared to the previous semester. A reporter heard the day before yesterday that Cheng Kuanzheng, the principal of Wusong Middle School, said that the three schools moved to Jingye Middle School in Xiaodongmen to hold classes. It is inconvenient for municipal elementary schools to act independently and recruit students in different places. Therefore, schools that have suffered from the war (as of April) still include Pengpu, Pusong, Yinxiang, Caojing, Zhenru, and Yinhang six districts' Jieyuan, Meicun, Chendu, Zhuku, Yucai, Zhalu, Zhuhang, Pengcheng, Zhenru, Guanlong, Zhangcun, Yizhong, Yinhang, Zhixing, Shen, Zhouwan and other twenty-four schools, all silent and without a single student. It is now heard that the Japanese troops have withdrawn, and they are all preparing to go back and open school.

The result of bombing, burning, destroying, and looting of municipal elementary schools in the three districts of Zhabei, Jiangwan, and Wusong is that many have been completely destroyed. Even if they have not been completely eliminated, many have collapsed or been damaged. Nine out of ten households have been abandoned, and school-age children can be said to be extinct. Even if schools are opened, no one will come to school. In the future, when peace is achieved, and we plan to revive, there should be a scientific, comprehensive plan that meets the needs of society. Therefore, at the end of February, the administrative organs carefully planned a proper solution. Starting in May, the schools in the three districts will be temporarily closed. Although the writing says "closed", in reality it is "start", starting the first step in preparing for the construction of schools in the near future. The reporter thinks that the construction of schools and even all cultural construction in the war zone will certainly be greater and more spectacular than before the war. The great Chinese nation will never bow its head, submit, fear, or fail to revive because of foreign invaders. It is only a matter of time before the blood and flesh of loyal soldiers will fertilize the land in the war zone, blooming with splendid cultural flowers. The Shanghai Education Bureau sees the clues in the regulations for the closure of schools in the three districts. The regulations are as follows:

1. All municipal elementary schools in Zhabei, Jiangwan, and Wusong three districts (hereinafter referred to as the three districts) shall be temporarily closed in accordance with these measures, pending the Bureau's consideration of the local situation and gradual planning of the entire recovery plan.

2. The principals of the municipal elementary schools in the three districts shall complete the transfer clearly within one week from the date of the order, and the custodian appointed by the Education Bureau (hereinafter referred to as the custodian) shall temporarily receive and keep it.

3. After the principals of the municipal elementary schools in the three districts have completed the transfer clearly, they shall be temporarily suspended from their duties and await separate transfer. All school workers in each school, except for those who are retained after consideration, shall be dismissed.

4. The principals of the municipal elementary schools in the three districts shall follow the following regulations for the transfer procedures: A. The principals shall accompany the custodians to inspect the original school or the original school site and inform the custodian in detail whether the school buildings and bases are municipal property or rented property. B. The principals shall inform the custodians in detail of the names, ages, birthplaces, and guarantor's name, occupation, and address of the original school servants. C. The principals shall hand over the bases of the school buildings that were burned down, the remaining school buildings and school supplies, and the school property transferred to other places to the custodians for registration and reporting. D. If any school has a final account that has not been reported or the school district construction fund account is not clear, the principal shall be responsible for reporting or clearing it within a time limit. E. After the principals have completed the transfer clearly, they shall submit the transfer books signed and sealed by the custodians to the Education Bureau. F. These measures shall be implemented from the date of approval and promulgation.

The Ambition and Strength of Japanese Athletes (Part 2) 120

Translated by Jiang Huaiqing

Pole Vault and Low Hurdles: Nishida Shuhei in the pole vault has an excellent record of 4.15 meters, and there are several others who can reach a height of 4 meters. Minakuchi, a student at Meiji University, has a fastest time of 56 seconds in the 400-meter hurdles, truly a rare talent. Sumiyoshi Kosaku of Waseda University has a score of 3614.355 in the decathlon. In addition, there must be relay races included. The 400-meter record of 41.6 seconds was created by Inuma Kiyotoku, Sasaki, Ame Iwao, and Yoshioka Ryu.

400 Meters and High Jump: Other items worthy of pride include Nakajima Igai Taro of Waseda University in the 400 meters, his masterpiece being 49 seconds; Kimura Kazuo in the high jump, his best performance almost reaching a height of 3 meters; Oshima Kamakichi of Kansai University in the high jump and long jump; Kitamoto Masaji of Keio University in long-distance running; and Sanroku Yoshio, a graduate of Keio University, who holds the national high hurdle record. All are world-renowned.

All of the above athletes will attend the World Olympics this fall. Judging from their individual performances, they are confident that they will give a special performance, winning the highest score for Japan and shining the spirit of Great Japan sports to all countries in the world.

The Great Swimming Pool in Los Angeles: Japanese swimming ranked second in the 9th Dutch World Games. This time, the Japanese athletes are deeply accomplished, and there is a great possibility of winning international championships. The newly built Los Angeles swimming pool was built exquisitely and is rare in various countries because Mr. Nakagawa Kenzo, the Japanese consul in Los Angeles, had previously requested the opinion of the Japanese Olympic Committee. The famous aquatic heroes of various countries will compete in the magnificent swimming pool from August 6 to 13 to glory for their country.

Japan Defeated American Stars Last Year: Last August, Japan invited the American National Swimming All-Star Team to Japan. In a three-day confrontation with Japanese athletes at the Meiji Jingu Swimming Pool, the Japanese athletes defeated the American All-Star Team by a score of 40 to 23, which shocked the swimming circles of various countries at that time.

Makino's Amazing Masterpiece: The extraordinary masterpiece of Japanese athletes is the highest record of 10 minutes, 25 seconds, and 2 tenths of a second in the 800-meter freestyle for middle and long distances by Japanese athletes. However, in last year's Japan-US confrontation, Makino Masazo set a shocking world record of 10 minutes and 6.6 seconds. The American generals Krabbe, Little, and Wiegerte were all defeated by the 15-year-old young hero Makino, truly the first miracle man in the world.

Creating a Special Situation: In addition, the Japanese championship holder Yamamoto Haruo's 200-meter freestyle in 2 minutes, 15 seconds, and 4 tenths of a second, Minakuchi's 100-meter freestyle in 59.2 seconds, and the 800-meter relay swim in 9 minutes, 20 seconds, and 9 tenths of a second created by Meiji University athletes, and the 300-meter medley relay in 3 minutes and 31 seconds are all outstanding achievements. In the previous World Games, Japan lost to Sweden, Austria, and Germany, which were famous in the swimming world, by 18 to 45 points, second only to the championship America. With the great progress of Japanese athletes, they will definitely be able to create a special situation. At the moment, the Japan Aquatic Sports Association is still selecting diving and water polo teams, as well as female athletes, to participate in the World Games, which is currently underway.

Rowing: In addition to the two important items of track and field swimming, it is also planned to send two groups of rowing athletes, one group of four and one group of eight, who are currently training. In last year's rowing competition between Waseda and Keio Universities, Waseda won the eight-person championship, and Keio won the four-person championship. Now, the athletes from these two universities are about to represent Japan at the World Games, which will also add a lot of glory to Japan.

The Tenth World Games is at hand. The high-spirited and energetic Japanese athletes will cross the Pacific Ocean on a long expedition, carry forward, work hard, and strive to win the championship in the Tenth Olympic Games in the world. This is what everyone wishes and congratulates. (The End)

The Terrible Fall of the Lil Silver Market 121

New Low Price: 6 Mace, 9 Fen, 4 Li

Market Overview: This year, due to the current situation, unexpected news that could never be imagined has often occurred. This drop in foreign lil silver is truly unprecedented. It was expected that upon expiration, there would be a gradual recovery for use, but it went against this expectation. Not only was it unable to recover, but it continued to decline rapidly. If this continues without restraint, the financial world will face the hidden worry of having nothing to do, and various businesses will face the difficulty of cash flow. This is truly a great misfortune for merchants. Today is the Summer Solstice, and the silver and money businesses are closed.

Lil Silver Discount Price: The "Foreign Lil Silver" market sentiment changed in the morning, and the situation became very weak, and sellers became more active. As a result, it was one and a half li smaller than the lowest price of the previous morning, at 6 mace, 9 fen, 4 li, 8 hao, 7 hu, and a half. The afternoon market was even more dangerous, falling another 875, to 6 mace, 9 fen, 4 li, an unprecedented new low price. Due to the long-term loosening of silver credit, the "Silver Discount" market had abundant reserves, so the morning and afternoon silver discounts were always borrowed without interest, and there was no increase in the commission rate.

Subsidiary Coin Market: The morning and afternoon prices of Jiangnan small silver coins were both 5 mace, 9 fen, and 9 li, which was 1 and a half li smaller than the previous day. However, it also entered the 6 mace mark, mostly due to the fall in foreign lil silver. The transaction volume was 4,000 jiao in the morning market and unheard of in the afternoon market. Although Guangdong small silver coins did not have a huge drop yesterday, they were also reduced by about 1 li due to the foreign lil silver relationship. The morning market was 5 mace, 9 fen, 3 li, and 2 hao and a half, and the afternoon market was 5 mace, 9 fen, and 3 li and a hao and a half. The transaction volume was 235,000 jiao in the morning market and 90,000 jiao in the afternoon market. Steel dollars also deviated from the norm, and the price yesterday was 2,000 wen longer than the previous day, a new price of 425,500 wen, which is also an unprecedented event in the history of steel dollars.

Silver Dollar Inflow and Outflow: "Silver Funds" Yesterday, due to unstable market sentiment and the unfinished period after settlement, there were not many collections. Chinese merchants collected 2.3 to 2.4 million in ticket funds, foreign merchants collected 1.7 to 1.8 million in ticket funds, remittance collections were more than 1.1 million, cargo funds were more than 1.8 to 1.9 million, mortgage funds were more than 1.2 million, telegraphic transfers were more than 500,000, customs duties were also more than 500,000, miscellaneous collections were more than 2.8 to 2.9 million, foreign funds were more than 600,000, warehouse outflow was 900,000, money shop and silver guild single collections were more than 19 million, commission rate collections were more than 3.3 million, various remittance collections were more than 400,000, and cash collections were 400,000 to 500,000. "Foreign Funds" The morning market for remittance and ticket funds was 615,000, and the afternoon market was 475,000. Banknotes were 50,000 in the morning market and 20,000 in the afternoon market. Off-exchange banknotes were 160,000 in the morning market and 50,000 in the afternoon market. Bank trading in the morning market was 550,000 in mutual trading, and 400,000 in mutual trading in the afternoon market. The inflow and outflow of foreign accounts of various banks was more than 1.1 million, the inflow and outflow of banknotes was more than 1.1 million, the single collections of foreign guilds in money shops were more than 4.8 million, the foreign commission rate collections were more than 2.1 million, the inflow and outflow of foreign funds for borrowing was more than 1.2 million, and the transactions of small money shops in the inflow and outflow of banknotes and remittance commission were 400,000 to 500,000.

New York Stock Market Reacted and Fell Back 126

(Report from the American Eastern Bank Company)

New York on Monday presented a technical reaction, so the two-day rise has been slightly suppressed, and prices have also fallen back with public debt securities, but in the aftermarket, they have all tended to be firm. Industrial stocks fell by 1.56 pounds, which is slightly more serious, but Monday's reaction is purely technical. The only consumption that deserves attention on this day is the Senate's difficulty in resolving the issue of whether to include electricity tax in the tax bill, but according to the latest news, the entire tax bill has been passed by the Senate. Another phenomenon in the market on Monday is enough to prove that the reaction belongs to technical covering. Sellers in the aftermarket have almost disappeared, so the market is actively upward, and several stocks have even exceeded the height reached on the previous day, especially public utility stocks. Regarding the budget issue, the Senate passed the tax bill on the 6th. After the passage of this bill, the national tax revenue is expected to reach 111.9 million yuan, while the total expenditure is 112.5 million yuan. The shortage of 6 million yuan will be reduced from government expenses. The budget balance issue has been resolved, and the industrial and commercial circles will follow the banking circles to make constructive efforts. According to the news on the 6th, the White House has announced that it will increase the financial relief agency's capital to 300 million yuan, establish a domestic loan discount bank, and establish a financial and industrial mixed committee in accordance with the Federal Reserve system. With these kinds of plans, it is predictable that the recent rebound in the stock market will continue to progress. The Dow Jones Index on Monday is as follows:

Last week, American cotton was weak.

Europe and India Settle Accounts 130

New York, June 3rd dispatch: The cotton market situation for the week is as follows: This week, the raw cotton market has been weak due to a large number of settlements from Europe and India. Furthermore, the stock and commodity markets were also weak, making the cotton market even more sluggish. Although the July futures price fell below five cents, the market rebounded, rising by more than one dollar per bale. However, confidence is still lacking, and settlement activities are prevalent. News of extremely unsatisfactory domestic and foreign trade, as well as anxieties about political developments, have contributed to the weakness of the cotton market. The reports on climate and cotton crop conditions this week have been satisfactory. Many believe that the drop in cotton prices has consolidated the actual position. However, although demand from the trade has picked up at low prices, general buyers have expressed hesitation, anticipating that if the weather is favorable in June, local settlements may increase in July. At the same time, sentiment is uncertain, and everyone is closely watching developments on Wall Street and in Washington.

Wuxi Cocoon Merchants Freely Handling Drying for Farmers 132

Business Tax Exemption Granted

More Farmers Drying Cocoons Themselves Due to Low Cocoon Prices

Farmers in various cities and villages in Wuxi have suffered damage to their early and late silkworm crops this year due to weather conditions. Although new cocoons have been successively launched on the market, the overall cocoon production is only twenty to thirty percent of normal years. Only fifteen cocoon merchants have opened for business. Most silk mills in the urban area have scales set up to collect cocoons in front of their doors. Arrivals are gradually increasing, and most are limiting prices for cocoon purchases. The highest price for high-quality foreign varieties of cocoons is only around thirty yuan. More silkworm farmers are drying the cocoons themselves, and the cocoon merchants who have not opened for business are allowed to freely dry cocoons for farmers, with a one-year exemption from business tax.

Recently, the local foreign firm silk market has completely collapsed. Upon investigation, silk prices in the European and American markets have repeatedly plummeted, and telegrams regarding Chinese silk have been scarce. It is estimated that ten bales of Zhonghe Jima brand top-grade Qilibai dried silk were priced at only five hundred taels. Five bales of Samsung Jinzhou top-grade yellow silk were priced at four hundred and twenty taels. Local News

The Municipal Government Held an Extraordinary Meeting Yesterday

Discussing Three Important Cases 141

The Issue of Road Construction Beyond the Boundaries is Submitted to the Central Government for Review

The Construction of the City Center District is Decided to Continue in Jiangxi

Instructing the Finance Bureau to Raise 5 Million to Revitalize the War Zone

Yesterday afternoon at 4:00 PM, the Municipal Government of this city held an extraordinary municipal meeting. Attendees included Mayor Wu, Secretary-General Yu, the directors of various bureaus, and Councilor Yin Rugeng. The important items discussed included: (1) the issue of road construction beyond the boundaries; (2) the issue of the city center district; and (3) the issue of revitalizing the municipal administration in the war zone. Regarding the first item, the issue of road construction beyond the boundaries, because both parties had already signed and approved the outline of the draft agreement on the issue, in addition to Secretary-General Yu's report on the progress, the content of the articles was also studied and discussed in detail. As a result, an opinion letter was attached to the outline of the draft agreement and submitted to the Central Government for review. The second item, the construction of the city center district, was decided to continue the work. The third item, the issue of revitalizing the municipal administration, was decided to be carried out by the Municipal Finance Bureau raising 5 million to carry out. The discussion ended at 6:00 PM.

Negotiations for Road Construction Beyond the Boundaries

Attitudes of Various Related Countries 142

Except for Japan, Which Expressed Clear Opposition

The Others All Believe That the Resolution is Not a Problem

Xin Sheng News Agency reports that the Shanghai Municipal Government and the Public Concession Board have recently negotiated the issue of road construction beyond the boundaries of the Shanghai Public Concession. According to the official announcement of the authorities, a considerable stage has been reached, and it can be resolved after the two parties separately request instructions from the National Government and the Shanghai Consular Body. After receiving this report, the government will have a thorough consideration, and the Consular Body will also have considerable research. Therefore, the attitudes of the countries related to the Public Concession are of general concern. A reporter from Xin Sheng News Agency specifically inquired about everything from various related parties. The information obtained is recorded as follows:

British Side: British Administrative Consul Davidson is responsible for this matter. A reporter from Xin Sheng News Agency visited him twice, but was unable to meet him because he was attending the Hartung estate as a witness. Subsequently, because the British side regarded Marsel, the chairman of the British Chamber of Commerce, as more reputable, and he had also written to the Consular Body regarding the Roundtable Conference, requesting that it be convened as soon as possible, he was directly met at the Xiangxing Company. According to his conversation, the British side has no objection to resolving the issue of road construction beyond the boundaries. He believes that this matter is not a matter for the Consular Body and the Chinese government. To seek a resolution, Mayor Wu Tiecheng and the authorities of the Public Concession Board can handle it directly. In the future, if the Concession Board must wait for the collective deliberation of the Shanghai Consular Body, he is not prepared to make any suggestions. As for the report in the Continental Daily that he wrote to the Consular Body requesting that the Roundtable Conference be convened as soon as possible, he believes that this is also a fair suggestion, because the Roundtable Conference is not held solely for the events of China and Japan. Its scope includes the nature of discussing international events, that is, the Chinese National Government also announced that the Manchurian incident must be discussed. As for the so-called Shanghai by the city, etc., this statement is too strange, and he strongly disagrees. Finally, he stated that he has been in Shanghai for 27 years and is very familiar with everything in Shanghai. In addition, he discussed many other situations.

Other Countries: Other countries, except for Japan, which has already expressed extremely clear opposition, generally have no significant opinions. (1) According to the American Administrative Consul Mu Qiu, he has not yet obtained the detailed content regarding the upcoming resolution of road construction beyond the boundaries. It will probably be decided first by China and the Concession Board themselves. He has not heard of the Consular Body convening a meeting. It is difficult to say what attitude the American community in Shanghai will take on this matter. In short, this road is more important in the relationship between China and Japan, and the US seems to have no objection. (Note: The above refers specifically to North Sichuan Road.) (2) According to the Counselor of the Italian Legation, Ross, he does not yet know what attitude the Italian side will take. This matter has not yet been discussed. He believes that this kind of small matter does not require discussion or the expression of an attitude. (3) The Danish Consul General, Luo En, believes that this matter is not a big problem and should proceed in the same way as other countries. If a meeting of the Consular Body is convened to consider this matter, it will not be so early. It will probably be decided by Nanjing, etc.

Secret Deliberations of the Consular Body: Guowen News Agency reports that regarding the issue of road construction beyond the boundaries, since the Municipal Government and the Concession Board contacted each other, both parties have discussed specific measures and submitted them to their superiors for instructions. According to reliable sources yesterday, the draft agreement agreed upon by the two parties consists of a total of sixteen articles. The Consular Body is currently secretly discussing it these days, and it takes a lot of time to discuss the articles. It is heard that a public discussion will be convened by the consuls of various countries within this week in order to resolve the issue as soon as possible. As for our country, the original text of the draft is now being submitted for review, and it is also heard that it can be issued and announced within this week.

Negotiations for the Japanese Army to Withdraw Quickly 143

Yu Hongjun Denies Restoring Administration First

Regarding the issue of the Japanese army's withdrawal, since Okazaki, the Japanese committee member of the Joint Committee, notified our committee member Yu Hongjun by telephone the day before yesterday, informing him that he still needs to continue consulting with the Japanese naval authorities and asking for a little more time, Yu has not received any further indications from the Japanese side until last night. However, yesterday, all newspapers reported that before the Japanese side has a clear indication of the areas where the Japanese army has not withdrawn, we have decided to restore police power and administrative power in the two places first. This is a misunderstanding of rumors. Regarding the restoration of administrative power, a reporter from the Far East News Agency asked Committee Member Yu Hongjun the day before yesterday, and according to Committee Member Yu, the Japanese army's long delay in withdrawing has no basis at all. It is clear that they cannot violate the treaty of truce and station their troops in areas where they should not be stationed. Therefore, we can only urge them to withdraw in order to restore our administrative power as soon as possible, otherwise the Japanese army will be responsible for destroying the truce agreement. Yesterday, the reporter saw that the news in the newspaper was the opposite of Mr. Yu's statement, so he visited and asked Mr. Yu again about this news, and he strongly denied it. He said that when he met with Okazaki on the fourth, he criticized that the Japanese army would not withdraw for a day, and he could not exercise his power for a day. At that time, Okazaki said that we might as well restore the power first. But how can the exercise of power be under the authority of another country's army? Therefore, he immediately expressed his opposition at that time and strongly urged them to withdraw. In short, before the Japanese army completely withdraws, he will never send a policeman or an official to post in the administrative district. The reports in the newspapers may have some misunderstanding on this point.

Concession

Telephone Workers Strike 144

Suddenly Implemented at 7 PM Last Night

Eleven Demands Raised

Telephone Calls Not Affected

Yesterday, starting at 7:00 PM, the workers of the Shanghai Telephone Company suddenly declared a strike. After 7:00 PM last night, telephone service was disrupted in the French Concession and a part of the western district of the Public Concession. After repairs, it was fully restored at 9:00 PM. Telephone calls throughout the city were normal. According to workers' claims, about 3,000 telephone company workers participated in the strike unanimously. Their demands include increasing wages, improving treatment, and job security. The telephone company, on the other hand, said that only a part of the workers in the automatic machine room were on strike, which did not affect operations, and that the striking workers had not made any demands or notifications beforehand. Details are recorded as follows:

Course of the Strike: Since the Shanghai Telephone Company switched to automatic machines, it has reduced the number of workers many times, and the treatment has also been extremely difficult. In January of this year, there was brewing for a strike, and representatives were elected to contact the capitalists. Then the Shanghai war broke out, and it was shelved invisibly until now. A week ago, the workers once again made five demands to the capitalists, including increasing wages, improving treatment, and not dismissing workers. The capitalists did not give a satisfactory answer. Until 7:00 PM yesterday afternoon, when the workers on the night shift went to work, they suddenly announced a strike. The capitalists had not received any notice in advance.

Normal Telephone Calls: After the strike, none of the workers on the night shift went to the bureau to work, so the machine rooms and switchboards of the telephone bureaus in the British and French Concessions were unmanned. The bureau temporarily sent Western engineers to manage them. The telephone lines in the French Concession and the western district of the Public Concession were slightly damaged, causing temporary interruptions. All repairs were completed until 9:00 PM. Because the telephone is completely automatic, there were only more than 40 switchboard workers on the night shift in the entire city. Last night, each bureau was replaced by one or two Westerners, so telephone calls were still normal and were not affected by the strike.

Strike Declaration: The strike declaration of the workers of the Shanghai Telephone Company reads, "Workers and people of the whole of Shanghai, we telephone workers who are cruelly oppressed and exploited by the American imperialist Electric Trust. In order to increase profits, the capitalists desperately implement rationalized production, transform automatic machines, and lay off workers in large numbers. Every telephone worker feels extremely painful and can no longer bear it. In order to save our lives and livelihoods, we have united unanimously. There is really no second way except to wage a resolute struggle against the telephone capitalists. Since the September 18th Incident, Japan and all imperialists have intensified their attacks on China and divided China. The attacks by the so-called civilized American imperialist telephone capitalists on our telephone workers have become even more cruel. In the past few months, hundreds of our telephone workers have been dismissed and abandoned on the streets, and no one cares about them. Because many workers' families and houses were bombed and destroyed by Japanese imperialist planes and artillery during the Shanghai war, our telephone workers still disregarded their lives and worked as usual under the threat of artillery fire. Recently, the telephone capitalists wanted to dismiss more than 300 workers in June and hire White Russians to replace the work of Chinese workers. Not only did they dismiss workers in large numbers and increase work, but they also canceled the precedent of increasing wages in April every year, and also canceled Sunday work, etc. Many old employees who have worked in the company for more than ten or twenty years still have wages of only about 20 yuan. The savings that have been accumulated year by year are often deducted and confiscated by the capitalists for no reason. According to the workers in the engine room, the working hours are more than twelve hours. It is obvious that the more so-called 'civilized' and 'advanced' imperialist capitalists are, the more they are the most cruel vampires of our workers. Smart imperialist capitalists are afraid that we, the oppressed slaves, will rise up to fight, and have come up with many tricks to deceive us and oppress us, so that we all do not dare to move. All the worker traitors and running dogs have unanimously risen up to serve the capitalists, saying things like 'Don't strike if you are anti-imperialist', 'Don't be anti-imperialist if you strike', 'The imperialist capitalists have no choice but to dismiss workers', 'The telephone strike is disrupting the social order of Shanghai', and 'The telephone workers' struggle can only be waged after the whole of Shanghai's workers rise up to fight', etc., selling out the interests of the workers, dispersing our strength, and eliminating our struggle. The eighteen articles proposed by the trade union last year and the signature campaign initiated by the foreman recently have all become empty words on blank paper. This tells us that the peaceful method of not waging a fierce struggle against the capitalists has no result. It is helping the imperialist capitalists and selling out the interests of our workers. We telephone workers can no longer endure it. Past experiences have taught us that now we can only unite unanimously, rely on our own strength, and wage a resolute struggle against the imperialist capitalists to protect ourselves and improve our painful lives. Our purpose is to achieve our required conditions. We swear to resolutely implement a general strike to seek our victory, and not be subjected to any threats, oppression, deception, destruction, or devastation. We hope that all the workers and people of Shanghai will unanimously support us, and please provide assistance in spirit, material, and struggle strength. We, the workers of the whole of Shanghai, will work hand in hand on the same front to wage a resolute struggle against the imperialist capitalists. If our workers cannot endure it, we will definitely strike on June 7th. This is our declaration."

Demands: The strike conditions are as follows: (1) Oppose the dismissal of workers, oppose the increase of work, and restore the jobs of dismissed workers; (2) Increase wages uniformly for all workers, old and new (specific measures will be determined later), starting from April of this year; (3) Oppose the cancellation of Sunday work, and double the wages for work during holidays; (4) Return the savings to the employees for their own safekeeping; (5) Guarantee no dismissal when transferring jobs; (6) Pay wages as usual during sick leave, and do not dismiss workers after they recover; (7) The working hours of workers in the engine room should be the same as the working hours of ordinary workers; (8) Do not transfer workers in the automatic machine test lines to do odd jobs, such as sweeping the floor; (9) If the company needs to recruit employees, it should first be supplemented by unemployed telephone workers; (10) Oppose the employment of White Russians; (11) Oppose the telephone company increasing telephone charges to users.

Capitalist's Statement: A reporter from this newspaper interviewed Mr. Gail, the deputy director of the telephone company, last night. He said that the strike started at 7:00 PM and was only carried out by some workers on the night shift. There was no contact or notification with the authorities beforehand. As for the workers, they sent representatives to the authorities in January of this year to make some demands, but they have not been resolved. As for the purpose of the workers' demands, the company set up automatic machines, the need for employees is gradually decreasing, resulting in layoffs and deep anxiety, on the one hand, to increase wages, on the other hand, to require security, but in the company, in order to promote the general welfare of the people, so that users pay fees as much as possible to reduce, if the workers say, will use to increase the burden of telephone charges, and said that day shift workers whether to participate in the strike, did not dare to decide, because tomorrow (that is, today) is a holiday.

Company Notice: The Shanghai Telephone Company issued a notice last night stating that because some machine and switchboard workers have stopped working, users may experience slight delays when dialing 01 and 09, please forgive.

Recent Movements of the Japanese Navy 145

Marine Corps Inspected Yesterday: Uematsu, the commander of the Japanese naval marine corps, inspected the marine corps in Shanghai yesterday. The team of about 1,600 people, divided into infantry, tank team, howitzer team, machine gun team, gun carriage team, etc., gathered at Hongkou Park from Jiangwan Road to North Sichuan Road at 9:30 am. About 4,000 Japanese expatriates went to watch. At around 11:00 am, the team returned from North Sichuan Road to Wusong Road via Bazilu. The place where the army passed was guarded by armed marine corps, and pedestrians were generally prohibited. They could only pass after the army had passed.

Izumo Ship Scheduled to Leave Shanghai: Rear Admiral Shiozawa, commander of the First Overseas Dispatch Team of the Japanese Navy, has now been ordered to be reassigned as the director of the Naval Education Bureau. Rear Admiral Kikuno has been dispatched to succeed as the commander of the First Overseas Dispatch Team stationed in Shanghai. Also, the injuries of Nomura, commander of the Third Fleet, have gradually improved. Uematsu, commander of the Shanghai Marine Corps, has also been transferred back to his home country. Colonel Sugisaka has been appointed as his successor. Yesterday, the naval officers agreed to take the flagship Izumo ship on Saturday (11th) of this week and return to China. There are more than 700 naval personnel on the Izumo ship, who will also return to Japan with the ship at that time.

First Quarter of this Year

General Overview of Sino-American Trade 146

Decline in Chinese Exports to America

Increase in American Exports to China

Reports from the mainland state that, according to the latest trade report released by the U.S. Department of Commerce, the Open Door policy in Manchuria has, in reality, been closed. In the first three months of this year, American goods exported to Dalian were valued at only USD 293,000, a 35% decrease compared to the USD 450,000 during the same period last year. Conversely, during the same period, American goods imported to China (excluding Manchuria) totaled USD 20,327,000, a 25% increase compared to the USD 16,300,000 during the first three months of last year. Overall, the U.S. import trade has seen a decline this quarter, leading to a 58% decrease in goods exported from mainland China to the United States compared to the same period last year, valued at only USD 7,440,000. (Translator's note: This is only slightly more than one-third of the value of American imports. In other words, China's import surplus is twice its export value. With money flowing out like this, how can the people not be impoverished and wealth depleted? It is hoped that those who love to use foreign goods will pay close attention.) However, goods exported from Dalian to the United States increased by 22% compared to the same period last year, valued at USD 351,000. Furthermore, the total value of U.S. exports in the first three months of this year was USD 459,150,000, a 34% decrease compared to the same period last year (excluding the 25% increase in exports to China). The total value of imports was USD 397,850,000, a 29% decrease compared to the same period last year (note that the decrease in imports from China is even greater, reaching 58%, further illustrating the decline in China's exports to the U.S.). Moreover, the total value of U.S. foreign trade last year decreased by 25% compared to the previous year, and by 15% in the Far East. However, exports to China, including Hong Kong and Dalian, increased by 1%, while imports from China, including Hong Kong and Dalian, decreased by 31%. If China proper, Hong Kong, and Dalian are statistically separated, then American goods imported to China proper last year increased by 9% compared to the previous year, while Chinese goods exported to the U.S. decreased by 33%. In Dalian, American goods imported decreased by 66%, while Chinese goods exported to the U.S. decreased by 54%. In Hong Kong, American goods imported decreased by 18%, while Chinese goods exported to the U.S. increased by 9%. Although the import of American goods to Dalian and Hong Kong decreased significantly, the value of goods exported to China proper far exceeded that of the two ports, so after summing up, the total value of American goods exported to China last year still increased by 1% compared to the previous year.

Shao Lizi's Letter to Wang Xiaolai

Planning the Development of Resources in Gansu Province 147

Intending to Invite Entrepreneurs to Inspect

Shao Lizi, the chairman of Gansu Province, intends to devote effort to the development of resources in Gansu. Yesterday, he sent a letter to Wang Xiaolai, chairman of the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce, requesting that he invite entrepreneurs from Shanghai to inspect the province and promote the sale of domestic goods in the Northwest. Wang has sent a letter inquiring about the methods of contact. The correspondence is recorded below:

Shao Lizi's Letter: Your telegram arrived very late. I am deeply grateful for your kind words and congratulations. With my limited talent, I have been entrusted with a heavy responsibility, and I rely on the support of wise men from across the country. Gansu Province has suffered frequent disasters, and the people are impoverished. Villages are ruined, and fields are barren. The misery is worse than in any other disaster area. However, the customs are simple and honest, and the resources are abundant, making development possible. Entrepreneurs from Shanghai who are willing to engage in agriculture, mining, wool, leather, and other industries are welcome to inspect. Moreover, the shops in Shaanxi and Gansu provinces are filled with foreign goods, mostly transported from Tianjin. If merchants of domestic goods in Shanghai could pay attention to sending more samples and indicating methods of wholesale purchase, I am confident that Shaanxi and Gansu provinces could provide a large market. I hope you will strongly promote this. Furthermore, I have written to Mr. Ziqiao, asking him to solicit donations for the Gansu Province work relief projects and for resettling refugees in villages. I also ask for your support when you meet with him.

Wang Xiaolai's Reply: I have just received your letter. I deeply lament the difficulty of implementing policies in the aftermath of the destruction in Gansu Province. I am also inspired by the fact that the Qin and Long regions were once called treasure troves, awaiting development. I hope that people from the Southeast can work together to preserve resources for the country and open up opportunities for the people. This is truly the intention of a virtuous man. I will carefully discuss this with the industrial and commercial circles here and start by encouraging merchants to send samples and try sales. However, I need to know who to contact, whether there are any merchants in Lanzhou who can be entrusted with trial sales, or whether I should simply discuss this with the Lanzhou Chamber of Commerce. This is a new venture, and I would appreciate it if you could provide clear guidance so that we can follow it. As for agriculture, mining, wool, leather, and other industries, can you provide some general information so that it will be easier to gather entrepreneurs to come to Gansu for inspection? I have already conveyed your wishes to Mr. Zhu Ziqiao. Respectfully replied.

End of the Road for Traitors in the Zhenru District 155

Strange Kidnapping Case Remains Unresolved

When the Zhenru district in western Shanghai was occupied by the Japanese army, a town resident named Shen Songge, acting on the instructions of the Japanese side, organized a maintenance association and willingly became a puppet. As a result, everyone despised him. On the 23rd of last month, when our takeover committee went to take over the area, Shen disappeared suddenly on the afternoon of the same day. This has been going on for many days. The Public Security Bureau, based on a report from Shen's wife, Li, that her husband had been kidnapped by the local defense force, had Chief Wen Yingxing order the Criminal Investigation Division to arrest Fu Zhongmin and others, members of the force. However, the merchants and residents of the town believed that those arrested were innocent and wrongly accused, so they went on strike to help them. After the head of the town's defense force, Wang Shouyu, and Municipal Committee Member Hong Lanxiang went to the municipal government to bail them out the other day, the matter was brought to an end. However, the kidnapping case of the traitor Shen Songge has not yet been resolved. A reporter from the Huadong News Agency went to Zhenru yesterday to investigate the matter. The information obtained is recorded below: The Process of the Traitor's Kidnapping: According to Shen Songge's wife, Li, when her husband was kidnapped, she was still living in Shanghai. The kidnapping occurred at 1:00 PM on the 23rd. At that time, Shen Songge was at his residence in Nanyangzhai, north of Zhenru Town, with an old servant. When he was kidnapped, dozens of armed and plainclothes members of the local defense force first went to Shen's residence, claiming to borrow a door panel. When they saw Shen, they immediately arrested him and took him away, heading east. When Shen's old servant saw this, he knew something was wrong and followed them, hoping to find out what was going on. However, after walking only a few steps, he was stopped at gunpoint by the defense force members, who threatened to arrest him as well. The servant had no choice but to walk to Shanghai to report everything to his mistress, Li.

Shen's Wife Goes to the Rescue: After Li was informed by the old servant, she was shocked and immediately walked from Shanghai to Zhenru with the old servant. However, it was already dark, and they could not continue west from Caojiadu due to the curfew, so they stayed overnight at a relative's house. The next morning, they continued to move forward and arrived in town. First, they went to the office of Municipal Committee Member Hong Lanxiang, but Hong had gone to Shanghai. Then, they went to see Wang Shouyu, the head of the town's defense force, and reported the details. However, Wang firmly denied that the members of the force had arrested Shen and had a conflict with Li. The two parted unhappily. Li then visited Municipal Committee Member Hong Lanxiang again, but to no avail. However, according to Li, Hong had said that the defense force would not do such a thing and could help investigate as a friend. They agreed to meet again in three days to hear the news. Li had no choice but to return to her residence in Shanghai. Three days later, she visited again, but still had no news from Hong. Helpless, she reported the details to Shi Jinzhang, the director of the Fourth District Third Precinct of the local Public Security Bureau.

Report to the Municipal Public Security Bureau: There was also a reason for Li to report to the local Public Security Bureau. When Shen was arrested, his old servant had followed behind him. When a group of people surged out, they encountered the Ping'an Security Team stationed near the Zhenru railway station. Shen... shouted for help. The Ping'an Security Team... police... went to investigate... However, the defense... personnel... said this is... our business... you don't need to interfere... Your Director Shi... also knows about this. Therefore, Li went to report to the local precinct. However, Director Shi was not aware of this and was greatly surprised. He considered this a major matter and ordered Li to report to the Public Security Bureau in person. After Chief Wen heard about this, he believed that although the traitor was hateful, the local people could list the evidence and file a complaint with the authorities. How could they privately arrest him? Based on the report, he brought the witness and ordered the Criminal Investigation Division to arrest the related personnel, thus causing the strike in Zhenru Town.

Report from the Third Precinct of the Fourth District: Regarding this matter, a reporter from the Huadong News Agency went to investigate the Fourth Precinct Third Section. Director Shi Jinzhang was out, so they were received by Inspector Liu. According to Inspector Liu, the precinct was initially unaware of the incident when it occurred on the 23rd. After reporting, Director Shi visited Municipal Committee Member Hong Lanxiang. However, Hong claimed to be unaware of the matter. Later, the Pingjing police responsible for taking over the area reported witnessing the incident but were unable to stop it. Therefore, the clues in this matter are very suspicious. The precinct is now rigorously investigating the matter in the hope of finding out the truth.

A Bizarre Advertisement: After the incident, Shen Songge's wife, Li, received an anonymous letter from a kidnapper stating that the matter had nothing to do with the defense force and was done by their brothers. If they wanted Shen to return home safely, they had to pay a ransom of 30,000 yuan. The letter also stated that the contact method was to publish an advertisement according to the instructions in the letter. Li submitted the letter to the Public Security Bureau and was allowed to publish the advertisement. However, after it was published the other day, no one came to contact them, so Shen's whereabouts are still unknown. The wording of the advertisement is quite bizarre and is recorded below: "Nanyang Bamboo Shoot Company is buying genuine sweet soy sauce. If you have the above-mentioned goods, please send a letter to No. 2 Run'an Lane, Taiping Bridge, French Concession, stating the price, quantity, and the name and location of the contact person for our company to collect."

A Glimpse of the Traitor's Residence: Shen Songge's being a traitor is something that everyone hates and abhors. However, his sudden disappearance is also puzzling. When Shen was in the puppet organization, he forcibly seized the property of nearby residents. His residence was filled with items belonging to nearby residents, and even items from the school were taken as his own. Yesterday, the reporter went to Shen's residence to inspect it. The doors and windows of Shen's house had been destroyed by the residents. There was also a seal on the door posted by the staff of the railway station, stating that Shen was not allowed to open the door without permission if he returned home and had to contact the railway station staff, because Shen's house contained items from the railway station. Shen's residence was quite clean, as he was one of the more affluent people in the area.

Mr. Hong Lanxiang's Talk: According to Municipal Committee Member Hong Lanxiang of Zhenru District, speaking to the Huadong News Agency, Shen's kidnapping was actually done by local thugs who had been victimized by Shen when the Japanese army occupied the area and were now retaliating. It had nothing to do with the defense force, and they were never involved. When the incident occurred, I was in Shanghai. Now, there are false accusations against the force, which is unfortunate. This is because a certain local organization is at odds with the defense force. I am now submitting a request to the municipal government for a thorough investigation. Mr. Hong also cited an incident to prove his point, saying that if the defense force members were going to make a secret arrest, why would they be fully armed, giving people an opportunity? Furthermore, I was very close to Shen. His coming to live in the town, buying land, and... were all handled by me. How could such a thing happen? One day, the truth of this case will come to light and clear the force of false accusations. The defense force management committee has also dispatched personnel to thoroughly investigate the matter because it is so important.

Shen Jiayi

Discussing the Handling of Civil Enforcement Issues 162

Recently, foreign newspapers have frequently reported on issues involving the Special District Court's handling of civil enforcement. A reporter interviewed Shen Jiayi, President of the Second Branch of the Jiangsu Higher Court, about this matter. The conversation is recorded below: (Question) "Foreigners frequently complain about the Special District Court's handling of civil enforcement. What is the reason for this?" (Answer) "Enforcement is different from adjudication. Adjudication only investigates the facts and applies the law to seek a fair judgment. Enforcement, however, involves the defendant's financial resources, so adjudication is often easier than enforcement. This is not unique to China; it is the same in all countries. China's litigation law is modeled after the continental law system and adopts a three-trial system. Cases that go through two or three trials will naturally take a long time. If the defendant has not reached the level of bankruptcy and the plaintiff has not requested the court to declare provisional execution, provisional attachment, or provisional disposition according to the law, the defendant's property will not be subject to any restrictions. Those who intend to avoid enforcement can secretly transfer their property. This is also one of the difficulties of enforcement, which is unavoidable even in countries with more complete legal systems. In China, due to the incomplete registration and notarization systems, private property is even easier to conceal. These are all major reasons for the difficulty of enforcement. However, these are all related to the system or special circumstances, not to the court's inefficiency. I deeply know that the importance of judgment lies in enforcement, especially in swift enforcement. More than ten years ago, when I was the president of a local court, I felt that this matter should be given special attention, so I created a civil enforcement office to take on this responsibility. Since the establishment of the National Court, I have paid even more attention to this matter and have repeatedly instructed civil enforcement personnel to pay close attention to various practical matters to maintain the interests of creditors who have received judgments and to make judgments have consequences. Regarding the system, the Ministry of Judicial Administration is currently working on reforming the civil procedure and civil enforcement system, hoping to streamline procedures and benefit the parties involved." (Question) "Recently, foreigners have criticized the court, saying that there is unfairness in handling civil cases. Does the court have this issue?" (Answer) "As the president of the court, I do not want to argue about this kind of argument. However, China's current laws are all adopted from Europe and the United States, and judges must make judgments based on the law. Moreover, according to China's litigation law, a judgment must be written, listing the facts and reasons for the judgment. If there is anything inappropriate, it is easy to point it out. Therefore, it is not easy for a judge to make judgments with prejudice. If, within the scope of the law, the judge's judgment is favorable to the plaintiff or favorable to the defendant, it is extremely difficult to determine an absolute standard. It is too vague to simply say it is unfair. I very much hope that those who have doubts can cite specific judgments and ask legal scholars to publicly evaluate them, which would be very beneficial. In the past, foreign nationals in China sometimes used political power to achieve results in civil cases that exceeded the power of the law, such as civil cases in the old Mixed Court, where judgments were often final after only one trial, and debtors were detained even before a judgment was made. This is one example. This kind of effect is, of course, impossible to obtain in today's courts, which base their judgments and enforcement on the law. It would be a misunderstanding and even a suspicion of using politics to subjugate the law to blame the court for this inconvenience. Although the legal system may not be perfect, according to what I know, the Ministry of Justice is now working hard to carry out reforms to make it as perfect as possible. This is what I dare to announce to people both inside and outside the country."

Page 15

Recent News from the Xinwei Relief Society

The Shanghai Emergency Relief Association for Flood Disasters in Various Provinces and the Temporary Relief Association for Refugees in the War Zone, considering that the matters of emergency relief for flood disasters and relief for refugees had temporarily come to an end, jointly decided to announce their dissolution. However, given that there are still many displaced disaster victims and news of disasters in various provinces is constantly being heard, causing great pain and suffering, it was deemed inappropriate to simply ignore them. Therefore, a joint meeting of the two associations decided to organize the Xinwei Relief Society, which was officially established on June 1st to continue handling relief matters. The following information is recorded below:

Declaration: "The country is in trouble, and disasters are frequent. Floods are rampant, and foreign insults arrive. Those who are displaced have no one to turn to, and the flames of war come to an end. Alas, our children suffer this catastrophe. We are angry and heartbroken. We have established the Shanghai Emergency Relief Association for Flood Disasters in Various Provinces and the Shanghai Temporary Relief Association for Refugees in the War Zone, regardless of our limited resources. The Emergency Relief Association has allocated relief funds to nineteen provinces and cities, and the Relief Association has helped over 300,000 refugees. All of this relies on the enthusiastic assistance and generous contributions of people from all walks of life, which has made this charitable act possible. We are deeply grateful for this. Now that the emergency relief has been completed and the Shanghai war has ended, the two associations should be dissolved as soon as possible. Therefore, a joint general meeting was held, and it was unanimously agreed that the disasters, although said to be destiny, are actually due to poor human planning. Past relief efforts were all after-the-fact repairs, which were not very helpful. Therefore, learning from the past and being cautious in the future, rather than moving firewood after the disaster has arrived, it is better to bend the chimney in advance. Moreover, there are currently nearly 2,000 refugees in the relief association who have no home to return to, and the relief work in provinces that have not been completed by the Emergency Relief Association also needs to be properly planned. Therefore, the Xinwei Relief Society was initiated to eliminate passive methods and draw up a fundamental plan, based on loving people with virtue and helping people with law, so that they can each do their best and each achieve their lives. It is hoped that we can prepare for a rainy day and avoid digging a well when thirsty. However, this matter is significant, and we are willing to do our best, but we still hope that fathers, brothers, sisters, and aunts will have great compassion and provide spiritual and material support, so that planting melons will lead to melons and planting beans will lead to beans, believing in the evidence of cause and effect, and descending blessings and good fortune, surely rewarding those who give. We hereby declare, please consider carefully."

Articles of Association: "(Article 1) The purpose of this association is to provide relief to disaster-stricken compatriots using active methods so that they can each achieve their lives. (Article 2) This association will continue to handle relief matters from the Shanghai Emergency Relief Association for Flood Disasters in Various Provinces and the Shanghai Temporary Relief Association for Refugees in the War Zone in the Xinwei year. Therefore, it is named the Xinwei Relief Society. (Article 3) This association is initiated and organized by people from various charitable and public welfare organizations in Shanghai. Those who agree with the purpose of this association are all members of this association. (Article 4) The organization of this association is as follows: Executive Group, Audit Group, and Finance Group. Each group has a director and a deputy director, who are appointed by the board of directors. The organizational regulations and detailed rules of procedure will be determined separately. (Article 5)

This association may appoint several secretaries to handle various affairs. (Article 6) This association will hold a general meeting of members once a year, a board of directors meeting once a quarter, and a standing board of directors meeting once a month. Special meetings may be convened when necessary. (Article 7) The operating expenses and administrative expenses of this association will be raised by this association at any time. (Article 8) All income and expenditure of funds and goods will be publicly announced in the newspaper at any time. (Article 9) These articles of association will be reported to the National Government Relief Commission for record after being resolved by the general meeting. (Article 10) These articles can be changed.

Staff: Chairman of the Board Xu Jingren, Vice Chairman of the Board Wang Yiting, Standing Directors Wen Lanting, Xu Jingren, Wang Xiaolai, Zhang Xiaolin, Huang Hanzhi, Zhao Jinqing, Zhu Ziqiao, Wang Yiting, Chen Aishi, Qu Wenliu, Du Yuesheng. Executive Group Director Qu Wenliu, Deputy Director Huang Boduo. Audit Group Director Wen Lanting, Deputy Director Pan Gongdu. Finance Group Director Huang Hanzhi, Deputy Director Guan Yunnong.

Shanghai-Hangzhou National Highway to be Completed on Schedule 170

Trafficable by September 1st

The Shanghai-Hangzhou National Highway is an important highway for developing the industry and military transportation of Jiangsu and Zhejiang provinces. The National Government has ordered the governments of Jiangsu and Zhejiang provinces to build it as soon as possible. The construction of the road is now largely complete. The part belonging to Jiangsu Province, from Shanghai City, via Beiqiao (i.e., the new Shanghai County seat), Minhang, Nanqiao (Fengxian County seat), Jinshanwei, Jinshan County seat, to Zhaopu in Zhejiang, is about one hundred and several tens of kilometers long and will be completed in sequence. It is scheduled to be officially open to automobile traffic on September 1st. After that, in addition to the Shanghai-Hangzhou Railway, there will be another convenient route for transportation between Shanghai and Hangzhou.
